# Dolittle

## About this scanning module

According to Phil Stokes from SentinelOne, Dolittle is a Genieo variant, also known as MaxOfferDeal.
Phil Stokes' X post is not publicly available now, but [the Eclecgic Light Company blog states as follows](https://eclecticlight.co/2024/01/16/apple-has-just-released-updates-to-xprotect-and-xprotect-remediator-7/):

> However, XProtectâ€™s Yara definitions add one new detection rule for MACOS.DOLITTLE.HJK, and adjust the detection rule for MACOS.e79dc35. Many thanks to Phil Stokes @philofishal of SentinelOne Labs who has identified MACOS.DOLITTLE.HJK as detecting a Genieo variant, also known as MaxOfferDeal.

<details>
<summary>Remediation logic described with RemediationBuilder DSL (click to expand)</summary>
